***обуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обуть.html>обу́ть</a> (21610)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">об-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ob-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-уть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-utʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*obuti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обуть.html>обу́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обувать.html>обува́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to put shoes on somebody's feet, to help somebody put on his/her shoes
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обуть.html>обу́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́ги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obútʹ</b> nógi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put on shoes</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to provide with shoes</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to trick, to take in, to snooker</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">переобу́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pereobútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обух.html>обух</a> (21098)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">обухъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obuxŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*obuxъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обух.html>о́бух</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обух.html>обу́х</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">óbux</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obúx</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обух.html>о́буха</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обух.html>обуха́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обух.html>о́бухи</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обух.html>обухи́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обух.html>о́бухов</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обух.html>обухо́в</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">обушо́к</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>butt <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">the thicker end of a tool or a weapon, especially an axe</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плеть.html>пле́тью</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обух.html>о́буха</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> перешибёшь</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">plétʹju óbuxa ne perešibjóšʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">there is no use trying to fight against (or to win, overcome) somebody or something that is stronger than you</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обучаться.html>обуча́ться</a> (17047)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обучать.html>обуча́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obučátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***обучить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обучить.html>обучи́ть</a> (11851)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">об-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ob-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учить.html>учи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">učítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обучить.html>обучи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obučítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обучать.html>обуча́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учить.html>учи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to teach, to instruct, to train</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">об-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ob-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хвати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xvatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обхватить.html>обхвати́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obxvatítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обхватывать.html>обхва́тывать</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обхватывавший.html>обхва́тывавший</a> (26530)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обхватывавший.html>обхва́тывавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obxvátyvavšij</span>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обхватить.html>обхвати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obxvatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***обходительный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обходительный.html>обходи́тельный</a> (24701)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обходить.html>обходи́</a>(ться)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obxodí(tʹsja)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обходительный.html>обходи́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obxodítelʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>polite, courteous</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">обхожде́ние</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obxoždénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">об-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ob-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обходить.html>обходи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obxodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обойти.html>обойти́</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обходиться.html>обходи́ться</a> (4790)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обходить.html>обходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obxodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обходиться.html>обходи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obxodítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обойтись.html>обойти́сь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cost; to come to</li>
<li>to treat, to manage (with), to do (with), to make (with); to get by with (<a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> + instrumental case)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">usually in the negative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be able to do without
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>Без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:учебник.html>уче́бников</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:обходиться.html>обходи́ться</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Bez učébnikov ne <b>obxodítʹsja</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">One <b>cannot do without</b> textbooks.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́г</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:обходиться.html>обходи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:водка.html>во́дки</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On i dnjá ne móg <b>obxodítʹsja</b> bez vódki.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He <b>couldn't do</b> (even) a day <b>without</b> vodka.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to turn out, to work out</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обходить.html>обходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obxodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обшивка.html>обши́вка</a> (15241)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">обшива́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obšivátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обшивка.html>обши́вка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obšívka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обшивка.html>обши́вки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обшивка.html>обши́вки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обшивка.html>обши́вок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>edging, bordering</li>
<li>trimming</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">construction</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> boarding, panelling</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sheathing</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">shipbuilding</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> planking, plating
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наружный.html>нару́жная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обшивка.html>обши́вка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">narúžnaja obšívka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">skin-plating, ship's skin</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">aviation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> covering</li></ol>
